owes to the very illusion surrounding him. It is truly and literally as if the
attention of someone were <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> to a danger which had threatened him for
a <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> time, but of which he knew nothing. Hitherto he felt no fear, but
now that he knows, he is overcome by fear, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">though</span> the danger has not
been rendered greater by his knowing it.
The forces at <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">work</span> in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> are both destructive and constructive; the
destiny of manifested <span class="t0 t1 t15 t22 t25 t29 hoverable">beings</span> is birth and death. The seer is to <span class="t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t9 t11 t17 t18 t19 t20 t22 t26 hoverable">behold</span> the
working of these forces and the march of destiny. The veil enshrouding
the <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> in ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> is to be removed. But <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> is interwoven
with these forces and with this destiny. His own <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> harbors destructive
and constructive forces. His own <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> reveals itself to the seer as
undisguised as the other objects. He must not lose strength in the <span class="t3 hoverable">face</span> of
this self-knowledge; but strength will fail him unless he brings a surplus
on which to draw. For this purpose he must learn to maintain inner calm
and steadiness in the <span class="t3 hoverable">face</span> of difficult circumstances; he must cultivate a
strong trust in the beneficent powers of existence. He must be prepared to
<span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> that many motives which had actuated him hitherto will do so no
longer. He will have to recognize that previously he <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> and acted in a
certain <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> only because he was still in the throes of ignorance. Reasons
that influenced him formerly will now disappear. He often acted out of
vanity; he will now see how utterly futile all vanity is for the seer. He
often acted out of greed; he will now become aware how destructive all
greed is. He will have to develop quite new motives for his thoughts and
actions, and it is just for this purpose that courage and fearlessness are
required.
It is pre-eminently a question of cultivating this courage and this
fearlessness in the inmost depths of thought-life. The student must learn
never to despair over failure. He must be equal to the thought: I shall
forget that I have failed in this matter, and I shall try once more as <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">though</span>
this had not happened. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thus</span> he will struggle through to the firm
conviction that the fountain-head of strength from which he may draw is
inexhaustible. He struggles ever onward to the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> which will uplift him
and support him, however weak and impotent his earthly self may have
proved. He must be capable of pressing on to the future undismayed by
any experiences of the past. If the student has acquired these faculties up

38

to a certain point, he is then ripe to hear the real names of things, which
are the key to <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> knowledge. For initiation consists in this very act of
learning to <span class="t8 t13 t21 hoverable">call</span> the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> by those names which they bear in
the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> of their <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">divine</span> authors. In these, their names, lies the mystery of
things. It is for this <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> that the initiates <span class="t6 t9 t11 t19 t20 t22 hoverable">speak</span> a different language
from the uninitiated, for the former know the names by which the <span class="t0 t1 t15 t22 t25 t29 hoverable">beings</span>
themselves are <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> into existence.
In as far as initiation itself can be discussed, this will be done in the
following chapter.

39

III
Initiation
Initiation is the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t9 t10 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t22 t23 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">highest</span> stage in an esoteric training concerning which it is
possible to give some indications in a <span class="t6 t8 t10 t11 t16 t20 t21 t27 t28 hoverable">book</span> intended for the genuine
public. Whatever lives beyond forms a subject difficult to understand, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">yet</span>
the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> to it can be found by all who have passed through preparation,
enlightenment, and initiation as far as the lesser mysteries.
The <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and proficiency conferred by initiation cannot be obtained
in any other manner, except in some far distant future, after many
incarnations, by quite different means and in quite a different form. The
initiate of today undergoes experiences which <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> otherwise come to
him much later, under quite different circumstances.
The secrets of existence are only accessible to an extent corresponding to
man's own degree of maturity. For this <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> alone the path to the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span>
stages of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">power</span> is beset with obstacles. A firearm should
not be <span class="t0 t12 hoverable">used</span> until sufficient experience has been gained to avoid disaster,
caused by its use. A <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> initiated today <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> further ado <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> lack
the experience which he will gain during his future incarnations before he
can attain to <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> in the normal course of his development.
At the portal of initiation, therefore, this experience must be supplied in
some other way. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thus</span> the first instructions given to the candidate for
initiation serve as a substitute for these future experiences. These are the
so-called trials, which he has to undergo, and which constitute a normal
course of inner development resulting from due application to such
exercises as are described in the preceding chapters.
These trials are often discussed in books, but it is only natural that such
discussions should as a rule give quite false impressions of their nature;
for <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> passing through preparation and enlightenment no one can
know anything of these tests and appropriately describe them.
The would-be initiate must come into contact with certain <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> and facts
belonging to the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds, but he can only see and hear them if his
feeling is ripe for the perception of the <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> forms, colors and tones
described in the chapters on Preparation and Enlightenment.
The first trial consists in obtaining a truer vision than the average <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> has
of the corporeal attributes of lifeless things, and later of plants, animals
and <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> beings. This does not mean what at present is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> scientific
knowledge, for it is a question not of science but of vision. As a rule, the
would-be initiate proceeds to learn how the objects of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> and the
<span class="t0 t1 t15 t22 t25 t29 hoverable">beings</span> gifted with <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> manifest themselves to the <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> ear and the
40

spiritual eye. In a certain <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> these <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> then lie stripped — naked —
before the beholder. The qualities which can then be seen and <span class="t1 t2 t3 t6 t18 hoverable">heard</span> are
hidden from the <span class="t1 hoverable">physical</span> <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> and ears. For <span class="t1 hoverable">physical</span> perception they are
concealed as if by a veil, and the falling away of this veil for the would-be
initiate consists in a process designated as the process of Purification by
Fire. The first trial is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">therefore</span> known as the Fire-Trial.
For many people, ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> is itself a more or less unconscious process
of initiation through the Fire-Trial. Such <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> have passed through a
wealth of experience, so that their self-confidence, courage and fortitude
have been greatly strengthened in a normal manner while learning to bear
sorrow, disappointment and failure in their undertakings with greatness of
soul, and especially with equanimity and unbroken strength. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thus</span> they are
often initiates <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> knowing it, and it then needs but little to unseal
their <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> hearing and sight so that they become clairvoyant. For it
must be noted that a genuine fire-trial is not intended to satisfy the
curiosity of the candidate. It is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span> that he learns many uncommon <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span>
of which others can have no inkling, but this acquisition of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> is
not the end, but the means to the end; the end consists in the attainment,
thanks to this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> of the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds, of greater and truer selfconfidence, a <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> degree of courage, and a magnanimity and
perseverance such as cannot, as a rule, be acquired in the lower world.
The candidate may always turn back after the fire-trial. He will then
resume his life, strengthened in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> and soul, and wait for a future
incarnation to continue his initiation. In his present incarnation he will
prove himself a more useful member of <span class="t5 t11 hoverable">society</span> and of humanity than he
was before. In whatever position he may <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> himself, his firmness,
prudence, resoluteness, and his beneficent influence over his fellows will
have greatly increased.
But if, after completing the fire-trial, he should wish to continue the path,
a certain writing-system generally adopted in esoteric training must now
be revealed to him. The actual teachings manifest themselves in this
writing, because the hidden (occult) qualities of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> cannot be directly
expressed in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">words</span> of ordinary writing. The pupils of the initiates
translate the teachings into ordinary language as best they can. The occult
script reveals itself to the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> when the latter has attained <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span>
perception, for it is traced in the <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> and remains there for all
time. It cannot be learned as an artificial writing is learned and read. The
candidate grows into clairvoyant <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> in an appropriate way, and
during this growth in a new strength is developed in his soul, as a new
faculty, through which he feels himself impelled to decipher the
occurrences and the <span class="t0 t1 t15 t22 t25 t29 hoverable">beings</span> of the <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> like the characters of a
writing. This strength, with the experience it brings of the corresponding
trial, might possibly awaken in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> as <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">though</span> of its own accord, as the

41

soul continually develops, but it will be found safer to follow the
instructions of those who are spiritually experienced, and who have some
proficiency in deciphering the occult script.
The signs of the occult script are not arbitrarily invented; they correspond
to the forces actively engaged in the world. They teach us the language of
things. It becomes immediately apparent to the candidate that the signs he
is now learning correspond to the forms, colors, and tones which he
learned to perceive during his preparation and enlightenment. He realizes
that all he learned previously was only like learning to spell, and that he is
only now beginning to read in the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds. All the isolated figures,
tones, and colors reveal themselves to him now in one <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">great</span> connected
whole. Now for the first <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> he attains complete certainty in observing
the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds. Hitherto he could never know positively <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> he saw were rightly seen. A regular understanding, too, is now at
last possible between the candidate and the initiate in the spheres of <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span>
knowledge. For whatever <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> the intercourse between an initiate and
another <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> may <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">take</span> in ordinary life, the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> in its
immediate <span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> can only be imparted by the initiate in the abovementioned sign-language.
Thanks to this language the student also learns certain rules of conduct and
certain duties of which he formerly knew nothing. Having learned these he
is able to perform actions endowed with a significance and a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">meaning</span> such
as the actions of one not initiated can never possess. He acts out of the
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds. Instructions concerning such action can only be read and
understood in the writing in question.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Yet</span> it must be emphasized that there are <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> unconsciously gifted with
the ability and faculty of performing such actions, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">though</span> they have never
undergone an esoteric training. Such helpers of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> and of humanity
<span class="t2 t3 t4 t6 t11 t12 t19 t22 hoverable">pass</span> through <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> bestowing blessings and performing <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> deeds. For
reasons here not to be discussed, gifts have been bestowed on them which
appear supernatural. What distinguishes them from the candidate for
initiation is only that the latter acts consciously and with <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> insight into
the entire situation. He acquires by training the gifts bestowed on others
by <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> powers for the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> of humanity. We can sincerely revere these
favored of God; but we should not for this <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> regard the <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">work</span> of
esoteric training as superfluous.
Once the student has learned the sign-language there awaits him <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">yet</span>
another trial, to prove <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> he can move with freedom and assurance in
the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds. In ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> he is impelled to action by exterior
motives. He <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t7 t10 t11 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">works</span> at one occupation or another because one duty he is
impelled to action by exterior motives. He <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t7 t10 t11 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">works</span> at one occupation or
another because one duty or another is imposed on him by outward

42

circumstances. It need hardly be mentioned that the student must in no
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> neglect any of his duties in ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> because he is living and
working in <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds. There is no duty in a <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> that can force
a <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> to neglect any single one of his duties in the ordinary world. The
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">father</span> will remain just as <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">father</span> to his family, the mother just as
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> a mother, and neither the official nor the soldier, nor anyone else will
be diverted from his <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">work</span> by becoming an esoteric student. On the
contrary, all the qualities which make a <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> being capable and efficient
are enhanced in the student to a degree incomprehensible to the
uninitiated. If, in the <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> of the uninitiated, this does not always appear to
be the case, it is simply because he often lacks the ability to judge the
initiate correctly. The deeds of the latter are not always intelligible to the
former. But this only happens in special cases.
At this stage of initiation there are duties to be performed for which no
outward stimulus is given. The candidate will not be moved to action by
external pressure, but only through adherence to the rules of conduct
revealed to him in the occult script. He must now show in this <span class="t0 t2 t5 t13 t14 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">second</span> trial
that, led by such rules, he can act with the same firmness and precision
with which, for instance, an official performs the duties that belong to
him. For this purpose, and in the course of his further training, he will <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span>
himself faced by a certain definite task. He must perform some action in
consequence of observations made on the basis of what he has learned
during preparation and enlightenment. The <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> of this action can be
understood by means of the occult script with which he is now familiar. If
he recognizes his duty and acts rightly, his trial has been successful. The
success can be recognized in the alteration produced by his action in the
figures, colors, and tones apprehended by his <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> and ears. Exact
indications are given, as the training progresses, showing how these
figures appear and are experienced after the action has been performed,
and the candidate must know how to produce this change. This trial is
known as the Water-Trial, because in his activity in these <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds
the candidate is deprived of the support derived from outward
circumstances, as a swimmer is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> support when swimming in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">water</span>
that is beyond his depth. This activity must be repeated until the candidate
attains absolute poise and assurance.
The importance of this trial lies again in the acquisition of a quality.
Through his experiences in the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds, the candidate develops this
quality in a short <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> to such a <span class="t17 t29 hoverable">high</span> degree that he <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> otherwise have
to go through many incarnations, in the ordinary course of his
development, before he could acquire it to the same extent. It all centers
around the <span class="t7 t12 t13 hoverable">fact</span> that he must be guided only by the results of his <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span>
perception and reading of the occult script, in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> to produce the changes
in question in these <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> regions of existence. Should he, in the course
of his activity, introduce any of his own opinions and desires, or should he

43

diverge for one moment from the laws which he has recognized to be
right, in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> to follow his own willful inclination, then the result
produced <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> differ entirely from what was intended. He <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> lose
sight of the goal to which his action tended, and confusion <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> result.
Hence ample opportunity is given him in the course of this trial to develop
self-control. This is the <span class="t24 t25 hoverable">object</span> in view. Here again, this trial can be more
easily passed by those <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> life, before initiation, has led them to acquire
self-control. Anyone having acquired the faculty of following <span class="t17 t29 hoverable">high</span>
principles and ideals, while putting into the background all personal
predilection; anyone capable of always performing his duty, even <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">though</span>
inclinations and sympathies <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> like to seduce him from this duty —
such a <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> is unconsciously an initiate in the midst of ordinary life. He
will need but little to succeed in this particular trial. Indeed, a certain
measure of initiation <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">thus</span> unconsciously acquired in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> will, as a rule, be
indispensable for success in this <span class="t0 t2 t5 t13 t14 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">second</span> trial. For even as it is difficult for
those who have not learned to spell correctly in their childhood to make
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">good</span> this deficiency when fully grown up, so too it is difficult to develop
the necessary degree of self-control at the moment of looking into the
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds, if this ability has not been acquired to a certain degree in
ordinary life. The objects of the <span class="t1 hoverable">physical</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">world</span> do not alter, whatever the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> of our wishes, desires, and inclinations. In the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds,
however, our wishes, desires, and inclinations are causes that produce
effects. If we wish to produce a particular effect in these worlds, we must
strictly follow the right rules and subdue every arbitrary impulse.
One <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> quality is of very special importance at this stage of initiation,
namely, an unquestionably sound judgment. Attention should be paid to
the training of this faculty during all the previous stages; for it now
remains to be proved <span class="t0 t5 t8 t10 t14 t15 t21 t24 t28 hoverable">whether</span> the candidate is shaping in a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> that shows
him to be fit for the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">truth</span> path of knowledge. Further progress is now only
possible if he is able to distinguish illusion, superstition, and everything
fantastic, from <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span> reality. This is, at first, more difficult to accomplish in
the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> stages of existence than in the lower. Every prejudice, every
cherished opinion with regard to the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> in question, must vanish; <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">truth</span>
alone must guide. There must be perfect readiness to abandon at once any
idea, opinion, or inclination when logical <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> demands it. Certainty in
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds is only likely to be attained when personal opinion is never
considered.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">People</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> mode of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> tends to fancifulness and superstition can
never make progress on the path to <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> knowledge. It is indeed a
precious treasure that the student is to acquire. All doubt regarding the
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds is removed from him. With all their laws they reveal
themselves to his gaze. But he cannot acquire this treasure so <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as he is
the prey of fancies and illusions. It <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> indeed be fatal if his
imagination and his prejudices ran away with his intellect. Dreamers and

44

fantastical <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> are as unfit for the path to <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> as
superstitious people. This cannot be over-emphasized. For the most
dangerous enemies on the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> of the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds lurk in
such fantastical reveries and superstitions. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Yet</span> no one need to believe that
the student loses all <span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> of poetry in life, all <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">power</span> of enthusiasm
because the words: You must be rid of all prejudice, are <span class="t2 t11 t15 t19 t25 t27 hoverable">written</span> over the
portal leading to the <span class="t0 t2 t5 t13 t14 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">second</span> trial of initiation, and because over the portal
at the entrance to the first trial he read: <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Without</span> normal common <span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> all
<span class="t2 t3 t6 t18 hoverable">thine</span> efforts are in vain.
If the candidate is in this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> sufficiently advanced, a <span class="t26 hoverable">third</span> trial awaits
him. He finds here no definite goal to be reached. All is <span class="t1 t7 t12 t29 hoverable">left</span> in his own
hands. He finds himself in a situation where nothing impels him to act. He
must <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> his <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> all alone and out of himself. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Things</span> or <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> to
stimulate him to action are non-existent. Nothing and nobody can give him
the strength he needs but he himself alone. Failure to <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> this inner
strength will leave him standing where he was. Few of those, however,
who have successfully passed the previous trials will fail to <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> the
necessary strength at this point. Either they will have turned back already
or they succeed at this point also. All that the candidate requires is the
ability to come quickly to terms with himself, for he must here <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> his
<span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> self in the truest <span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> of the word. He must rapidly decide in all
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> to listen to the inspiration of the spirit. There is no <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> for doubt or
hesitation. Every moment of hesitation <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> prove that he was still unfit.
Whatever prevents him from listening to the voice of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> must be
courageously overcome. It is a question of showing presence of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> in
this situation, and the training at this stage is concerned with the perfect
development of this quality. All the accustomed inducements to act or
even to think now cease. In <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> not to remain inactive he must not lose
himself, for only <span class="t0 t1 t4 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">within</span> himself can he <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> the one central point of
vantage where he can gain a firm hold. No one on reading this, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span>
further acquaintance with these mattes, should feel an antipathy for this
principle of being thrown back on oneself, for success in this trial brings
with it a moment of supreme happiness.
At this stage, no less than at the others, ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> is itself an esoteric
training for many. For anyone having reached the point of being able,
when suddenly confronted with some task or problem in life, to come to a
swift decision <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> hesitation or delay, for him <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> itself has been a
training in this sense. Such situations are here meant in which success is
instantly lost if action is not rapid. A <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> who is quick to act when a
misfortune is imminent, whereas a few moments of hesitation <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> have
seen the misfortune an accomplished fact, and who has turned this ability
into a permanent personal quality, has unconsciously acquired the degree
of maturity necessary for the <span class="t26 hoverable">third</span> trial. For at this stage everything centers
round the development of absolute presence of mind. This trial is known

45

as the Air-Trial, because while undergoing it the candidate can support
himself neither <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the firm basis of external incentive nor <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the
figures, tones, and colors which he has learned at the stages of preparation
and enlightenment, but exclusively <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> himself.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Upon</span> successfully passing this trial the student is permitted to enter the
temple of <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> wisdom. All that is here said on this subject can only be
the slenderest allusion. The task now to be performed is often expressed in
the statement that the student must <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">take</span> an oath never to betray anything
he has learned. These expressions, however, “oath” and “betray”, are
inappropriate and actually misleading. There is no question of an oath in
the ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> of the word, but rather of an experience that comes at
this stage of development. The candidate learns how to apply the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span>
knowledge, how to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> it at the service of humanity. He then begins
really and truly to understand the world. It is not so much a question of
withholding the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> truths, but far more of serving them in the right
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> and with the necessary tact. The silence he is to keep refers to
something quite different. He acquires this fine quality with regard to
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> he had previously spoken, and especially with regard to the manner
in which they were spoken. He <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> be a poor initiate who did not <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span>
all the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> he had acquired at the service of humanity, as
<span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">well</span> and as far as this is possible. The only obstacle to giving information
in these matters is the lack of understanding on the part of the recipients. It
is true, of course, that the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> does not lend itself to
promiscuous talk; but no one having reached the stage of development
described above is actually forbidden to say anything. No other person, no
being exacts an oath from him with this intent. Everything is <span class="t1 t7 t12 t29 hoverable">left</span> to his
own responsibility, and he learns in every situation to discover <span class="t0 t1 t4 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">within</span>
himself what he has to do, and an oath means nothing more than that he
has been found qualified to be entrusted with such a responsibility.
If the candidate is found fit for the foregoing experiences, he is then given
what is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> symbolically the draught of forgetfulness. This means that
he is initiated into the secret <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> that enables him to act <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span>
being continually disturbed by the lower memory. This is necessary for the
initiate, for he must have <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> <span class="t7 t13 t19 t20 t29 hoverable">faith</span> in the immediate present. He must be
able to destroy the veil of memory which envelops <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> every moment of
his life. If we judge something that happens to us today according to the
experience of yesterday, we are exposed to a multitude of errors. Of
course this does not mean that experience gained in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> should be
renounced. It should always be kept in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> as clearly as possible. But the
initiate must have the ability to judge every new experience wholly
according to what is inherent in it, and let it react <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> him, unobscurred
by the past. We must be prepared at every moment that every <span class="t24 t25 hoverable">object</span> and
every being can <span class="t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t17 t18 t19 t20 t22 t23 t27 t29 hoverable">bring</span> to us some new revelation. If we judge the new by
the standard of the old we are liable to error. The memory of past

46

experiences will be of greatest <span class="t1 hoverable">use</span> for the very <span class="t1 t11 t16 t20 t25 t27 t28 hoverable">reason</span> that it enables us to
perceive the new. Had we not gone through a definite experience we
should perhaps be blind to the qualities of the <span class="t24 t25 hoverable">object</span> or being that comes
before us. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thus</span> experience should serve the purpose of perceiving the new
and not of judging it by the standard of the old. In this respect the initiate
acquires certain definite qualities, and thereby many <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> are revealed to
him which remain concealed from the uninitiated.
The <span class="t0 t2 t5 t13 t14 t16 t17 t20 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">second</span> draught presented to the initiate is the draught of
remembrance. Through its agency he acquires the faculty of retaining the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> of the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> truths ever present in his soul. Ordinary memory
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> be unequal to this task. We must unite ourselves and become as one
with the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> truths.
We must not only know them, but be able, quite as a matter of course, to
manifest and administer them in living actions, even as we ordinarily <span class="t6 hoverable">eat</span>
and drink. They must become our practice, our habit, our inclination.
There must be no need to keep thinking about them in the ordinary sense;
they must come to living expression through <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> himself; they must flow
through him as the functions of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> through his organism. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thus</span> doth <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span>
ever raise himself, in a <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> sense, to that same stature to which
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> raised him in a <span class="t1 hoverable">physical</span> sense.

47

IV
Some Practical Aspects
The training of thoughts and feelings, pursued in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> described in the
chapters on Preparation, Enlightenment, and Initiation, introduces into the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> the same organic symmetry with which <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> has
constructed the <span class="t1 hoverable">physical</span> body. Before this development, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> are
undifferentiated masses. The clairvoyant perceives them as interlacing,
rotating, cloud-like spirals, dully glimmering in reddish, reddish-brown, or
reddish-yellow tones. After this training they begin to assume a brilliant
yellowish-green, or greenish-blue color, and show a regular structure. This
inner regularity leading to <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> knowledge, is attained when the student
introduces into his thoughts and feelings the same orderly system with
which <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span> has endowed his bodily organs that enable him to see, hear,
digest, breath, speak. Gradually he learns to breath and see with this soul,
to <span class="t6 t9 t11 t19 t20 t22 hoverable">speak</span> and hear with the spirit.
In the following pages some practical aspects of the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> education of
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> will be treated in greater detail. They are such that anyone
can put them into practice regardless of other rules, and thereby be led
some distance further into <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> science.
A particular effort must be made to cultivate the quality of patience. Every
symptom of impatience produces a paralyzing, even a destructive effect on
the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> faculties that slumber in us. We must not expect an
immeasurable <span class="t25 hoverable">view</span> into the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> worlds from one <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">day</span> to the next, for we
should assuredly be disappointed. Contentment with the smallest fragment
attained, repose and tranquility, must more and more <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">take</span> possession of
the soul. It is quite understandable that the student should await results
with impatience; but he will achieve nothing so <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as he fails to <span class="t0 t1 t8 t11 t15 t21 t23 t24 hoverable">master</span>
this impatience. Nor is it of any <span class="t1 hoverable">use</span> to combat this impatience merely in
the ordinary sense, for it will become only that much stronger. We overlook it in self-deception while it plants itself all the more firmly in the
depths of the soul. It is only when we ever and again surrender ourselves
to a certain definite thought, making it absolutely our own, that any results
can be attained. This <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> is as follows: I must certainly do everything I
can for the training and development of my <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> and spirit; but I shall wait
patiently until <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> powers shall have found me worthy of definite
enlightenment. If this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> becomes so powerful in the student that it
grows into an actual feature of his character, he is treading the right path.
This feature soon sets its mark on his exterior. The gaze of his eye
becomes steady, the movement of his <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> becomes sure, his decisions
definite, and all that goes under the name of nervousness gradually
disappears. Rules that appear trifling and insignificant must be <span class="t2 t5 t11 t18 t19 t23 t26 hoverable">taken</span> into
account. For example, supposing someone affronts us. Before our training
48

we should have directed our resentment against the offender; a wave of
anger <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> have surged up <span class="t0 t1 t4 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">within</span> us. In a similar case, however, the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> is immediately present in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> of the student that such an
affront makes no difference to his intrinsic worth. And he does whatever
must be done to meet the affront with calm and composure, and not in a
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spirit</span> of anger. Of course it is not a <span class="t5 t16 t21 t24 t25 hoverable">case</span> of simply accepting every affront,
but of acting with the same calm composure when dealing with an affront
against our own <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> as we <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> if the affront were directed against
another person, in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">whose</span> favor we had the right to intervene. It must
always be remembered that this training is not carried out in crude
outward processes, but in subtle, silent alterations in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span>
and feeling.
Patience has the effect of attraction, impatience the effect of repulsion on
the treasures of <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> knowledge. In the <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> regions of existence
nothing can be attained by haste and unrest. Above all things, <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> and
craving must be silenced, for these are qualities of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> before which
all <span class="t0 t1 t11 t12 t21 t25 hoverable">higher</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> shyly withdraws. However precious this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span>
is accounted, the student must not crave it if he wishes to attain it. If he
wishes to have it for his own sake, he will never attain it. This requires
him to be honest with himself in his innermost soul. He must in no <span class="t5 t16 t21 t24 t25 hoverable">case</span> be
under any illusion concerning his own self. With a feeling of inner <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">truth</span> he
must look his own faults, weaknesses, and unfitness <span class="t10 t16 hoverable">full</span> in the face. The
moment he tries to excuse to himself any of his weaknesses, he has placed
a stone in his <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> on the path which is to lead him upward. Such obstacles
can only be removed by self-enlightenment. There is only one <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> to get
rid of faults and failings, and that is by a clear recognition of them.
Everything slumbers in the <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> and can be awakened. A <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span>
can even improve his intellect and reason, if he quietly and calmly makes
it clear to himself why he is weak in this respect. Such self- <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> is,
of course, difficult, for the temptation to self-deception is immeasurably
great. Anyone making a habit of being truthful with himself opens the
portal leading to a deeper insight.
All curiosity must fall away from the student. He must rid himself as much
as possible of the habit of asking questions merely for the sake of
gratifying a selfish thirst for knowledge. He must only ask when
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> can serve to perfect his own being in the service of evolution.
Nevertheless, his delight in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and his devotion to it should in no
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> be hampered. He should listen devoutly to all that contributes to such
an end, and should seek every opportunity for such devotional attention.
Special attention must be paid in esoteric training to the education of the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> of desires. This does not mean that we are to become <span class="t1 t8 hoverable">free</span> of desire, for
if we are to attain something we must also <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> it, and <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> will always
tend to fulfillment if backed by a particular force. This force is derived

49

from a right knowledge. Do not <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> at all until you know what is right
in any one sphere. That is one of the golden rules for the student. The <span class="t5 t8 hoverable">wise</span>
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">man</span> first ascertains the laws of the world, and then his desires become
powers which realize themselves. The following example brings this out
clearly. There are certainly many <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> who <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">would</span> like to learn from
their own observation something about their <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> before birth. Such a
<span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> is altogether useless and leads to no result so <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as the <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> in
question has not acquired a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> of the laws that govern the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span>
of the eternal, a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> of these laws in their subtlest and most
intimate character, through the study of <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> science. But if, having
really acquired this knowledge, he wishes to proceed further, his desire,
now ennobled and purified, will enable him to do so.
It is also no <span class="t1 hoverable">use</span> saying: I particularly wish to examine my previous life,
and shall study only for this purpose. We must rather be capable of
abandoning this desire, of eliminating it altogether, and of studying, at
first, with no such intention. We should cultivate a feeling of joy and
devotion for what we learn, with no <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> of the above end in view. We
should learn to cherish and foster a particular <span class="t0 t10 t11 t17 t25 t28 t29 hoverable">desire</span> in such a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> that it
brings with it its own fulfillment.
If we become angered, vexed or annoyed, we erect a wall around
ourselves in the soul-world, and the forces which are to develop the <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span>
of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> cannot approach. For instance, if a <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> angers me he sends
forth a psychic current into the soul-world. I cannot see this current as
<span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as I am myself capable of anger. My own anger conceals it from me.
We must not, however, suppose that when we are <span class="t1 t8 hoverable">free</span> from anger we shall
immediately have a psychic (astral) vision. For this purpose an organ of
vision must have been developed in the soul. The beginnings of such an
organ are latent in every <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> being, but remain ineffective as <span class="t0 t1 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">long</span> as he
is capable of anger. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Yet</span> this organ is not immediately present the moment
anger has been combated to a small extent. We must rather persevere in
this combating of anger and proceed patiently on our way; then some <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">day</span>
we shall <span class="t5 t14 t15 t24 t27 hoverable">find</span> that this eye of the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> has become developed. Of course,
anger is not the only failing to be combated for the attainment of this end.
Many grow impatient or skeptical, because they have for <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">years</span> combated
certain qualities, and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">yet</span> clairvoyance has not ensued. In that <span class="t5 t16 t21 t24 t25 hoverable">case</span> they
have just trained some qualities and allowed others to run riot. The gift of
clairvoyance only manifests itself when all those qualities which stunt the
growth of the latent faculties are suppressed. Undoubtedly, the beginnings
of such seeing and hearing may appear at an earlier period, but these are
only young and tender shoots which are subjected to all possible error, and
which, if not carefully tended and guarded, may quickly die.
Other qualities which, like anger and vexation, have to be combated, are
timidity, superstition, prejudice, vanity and ambition, curiosity, the mania

50

for imparting information, and the making of distinctions in <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">human</span> <span class="t0 t1 t15 t22 t25 t29 hoverable">beings</span>
according to the outward characteristics of rank, sex, race, and so forth. In
our <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> it is difficult for <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">people</span> to understand how the combating of such
qualities can have anything to do with the heightening of the faculty of
cognition. But every <span class="t0 t4 t6 t7 t8 t11 t14 t16 t17 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">spiritual</span> scientist knows that much more depends
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> such matters than <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the increase of <span class="t5 t15 t21 t27 hoverable">intelligence</span> and employment
of artificial exercises. Especially can misunderstanding arise if we believe
that we must become foolhardy in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> to be fearless; that we must close
our <span class="t2 t6 t19 t20 t26 t29 hoverable">eyes</span> to the differences between people, because we must combat the
prejudices of rank, race, and so forth. Rather is it <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span> that a correct
estimate of all <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">things</span> is to be attained only when we are no longer
entangled in prejudice. Even in the ordinary <span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> it is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span> that the <span class="t9 t19 hoverable">fear</span> of
some phenomenon prevents us from estimating it rightly; that a racial
prejudice prevents us from seeing into a man's soul. It is this ordinary
<span class="t0 t1 t7 t12 t13 t14 t17 t23 t27 t28 hoverable">sense</span> that the student must develop in all its delicacy and subtlety.
Every <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">word</span> spoken <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> having been thoroughly purged in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> is a
stone thrown in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> of esoteric training. And here something must be
considered which can only be explained by giving an example. If anything
be said to which we must reply, we must be careful to consider the
speaker's opinion, feeling, and even his prejudice, rather than what we
ourselves have to say at the moment on the subject under discussion. In
this example a refined quality of tact is indicated, to the cultivation of
which the student must devote his care. He must learn to judge what
importance it may have for the other <span class="t0 t4 t5 t10 t22 t25 t28 hoverable">person</span> if he opposes the latter's
opinion with his own. This does not mean that he must withhold his
opinion. There can be no question of that. But he must listen to the speaker
as carefully and as attentively as he possibly can and let his reply derive its
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> from what he has just heard. In such cases one particular <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span>
recurs ever and again to the student, and he is treading the right path if this
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> lives with him to the extent of becoming a trait of his character.
This <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">thought</span> is as follows: The importance lies not in the difference of our
opinions but in his discovering through his own effort what is right if I
contribute something toward it. Thoughts of this and of a similar <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">nature</span>
cause the character and the behavior of the student to be permeated with a
quality of gentleness, which is one of the chief means <span class="t0 t12 hoverable">used</span> in all esoteric
training. Harshness scares away the soul-pictures that should open the eye
of the soul; gentleness clears the obstacles away and unseals the inner
organs.
Along with gentleness, another quality will presently be developed in the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> of the student: that of quietly paying attention to all the subtleties in
the soul-life of his environment, while reducing to absolute silence any
